Rajdhani Medium Regular (Rajdhani-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Rajdhani' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Rajdhani Medium'.

OK: Font has both Typographic Family Name (NID 16) and Typographic Subfamily Name (NID 17).

Rajdhani SemiBold Regular (Rajdhani-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Rajdhani' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Rajdhani SemiBold'.

Pass

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '

NID 6 is 'Rajdhani-Bold', Everything looks good.

This Font Software is licensed under the SIL Open Font License, Version 1.1. This license is available with a FAQ at: http://scripts.sil.org/OFL
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. GPOS table does not have kerning feature. Please investigate if this meets requirements.

Info

Rajdhani Bold (Rajdhani-Bold.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in font.

Font has no 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Is longer:
'uni0915094D0937094D092E094D092F

uni0928094D0938094D092E094D092F
uni0924094D0930094D0915.aTrad'
